    <script>
      <!-- /* OneTrust callback */ -->
      function OptanonWrapper() {
        function getCookie(name) {
          var value = "; " + document.cookie;
          var parts = value.split("; " + name + "=");
          if (parts.length == 2) {
            return parts.pop().split(";").shift();
          }
        }
        function removeElement(element) {
          if (!getCookie('OptanonAlertBoxClosed') && element) {
            element.style.display = "none";
          }
        }
        <!-- /* enable footer link */ -->

        var footerLinkToggle = (document.querySelector(".page-footer_link .optanon-toggle-display") ? document.querySelector(".page-footer_link .optanon-toggle-display") : false);

        if (footerLinkToggle) {
          footerLinkToggle.addEventListener("click", Optanon.ToggleInfoDisplay, false);
          footerLinkToggle.addEventListener("keydown", function(e){
            if (e.keyCode === 13) {
              Optanon.ToggleInfoDisplay()
            }
          }, false);
        }
        //Check if user's cookies are enabled, if not remove One Trust from page
        var cookies = ("cookie" in document && (document.cookie.length > 0 || (document.cookie = "test").indexOf.call(document.cookie, "test") > -1));
        if (!cookies) {
          var box = document.querySelector('#onetrust-consent-sdk');
          box.remove();
          return;
        }
        try {
          //Check if current page is Privacy page, if so do not display One Trust modal
          if(digitalData) {
            if(digitalData.page.pagename.indexOf(":company:privacy") > -1){
              var el = document.querySelector("#onetrust-consent-sdk");
              removeElement(el);
            }
          }
          <!-- /* reinitialize active groups after user updates consent */ -->
          if (SfdcWwwBase.gdpr) {
            SfdcWwwBase.gdpr.init();
          }
        }catch(err){
          console.error(err.message)
        }
      }
    </script>

     $CQ(function() {
         var campaignParam = 'campaign',
             experienceParam = 'experience',
             campaignName = CQ.shared.HTTP.getParameter(location.href, campaignParam),
             experienceName = CQ.shared.HTTP.getParameter(location.href, experienceParam),
             allTeasers = [{"path":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage/customer-profile/home-columncontainer_5a3c","name":"home-columncontainer_5a3c","title":"jumbotron-news-ticker","campaignName":"homepage","campaignPath":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage","thumbnail":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage/customer-profile/home-columncontainer_5a3c.thumb.png","id":"homepage_home-columncontainer_5a3c","url":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage/customer-profile/home-columncontainer_5a3c/_jcr_content/par.html","campaignPriority":100,"segments":["/etc/segmentation/sfdc-www/customer-profile"],"tags":[]},{"path":"/content/www/en_us/home/jcr:content/main-par/columncontainer_5a3c/default","url":"/content/www/en_us/home/jcr:content/main-par/columncontainer_5a3c.default.html","name":"default","title":"Default","campainName":"","thumbnail":"/_jcr_content/main-par/columncontainer_5a3c/.thumb.png"}];

         // if campaign and experience in url params
         // get the specified experience and set it as the default in the allTeasers array
         if (campaignName && experienceName){
             function isForcedTeaser(teaser, campaign, experience){
                 var campaignsDirectory = '/content/campaigns';
                 var pathToCampaign = campaignsDirectory + '/' + campaign;
                 var fullPathToExperience = pathToCampaign + '/' + experience + '/';
                 if(teaser.campaignPath == pathToCampaign){
                     if(teaser.path.startsWith(fullPathToExperience) || teaser.thumbnail.startsWith(fullPathToExperience)){
                         return true;
                     }
                 }
                 return false;
             }
             
             for (i = 0; i < allTeasers.length; i++) {
                 if (isForcedTeaser(allTeasers[i], campaignName, experienceName)) {
                     var forcedTeaser = allTeasers[i];
                     forcedTeaser.name = "default";
                     forcedTeaser.segments = undefined;
                     delete forcedTeaser.segments;
                     allTeasers = [forcedTeaser]; 
                 }
             }
         }
	 
             CQ_Analytics.Engine.loadTeaser({ targetID: "_content_www_en_us_home_jcr_content_main-par_columncontainer_5a3c", teasers: allTeasers, strategy: "", trackingURL: null});
	 });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
     $CQ(function() {
         var campaignParam = 'campaign',
             experienceParam = 'experience',
             campaignName = CQ.shared.HTTP.getParameter(location.href, campaignParam),
             experienceName = CQ.shared.HTTP.getParameter(location.href, experienceParam),
             allTeasers = [{"path":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage/customer-profile/home-columncontainer_5696","name":"home-columncontainer_5696","title":"jumbotron-news-ticker","campaignName":"homepage","campaignPath":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage","thumbnail":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage/customer-profile/home-columncontainer_5696.thumb.png","id":"homepage_home-columncontainer_5696","url":"/content/campaigns/en_us/master/homepage/customer-profile/home-columncontainer_5696/_jcr_content/par.html","campaignPriority":100,"segments":["/etc/segmentation/sfdc-www/customer-profile"],"tags":[]},{"path":"/content/www/en_us/home/jcr:content/main-par/columncontainer_5696/default","url":"/content/www/en_us/home/jcr:content/main-par/columncontainer_5696.default.html","name":"default","title":"Default","campainName":"","thumbnail":"/_jcr_content/main-par/columncontainer_5696/.thumb.png"}];

         // if campaign and experience in url params
         // get the specified experience and set it as the default in the allTeasers array
         if (campaignName && experienceName){
             function isForcedTeaser(teaser, campaign, experience){
                 var campaignsDirectory = '/content/campaigns';
                 var pathToCampaign = campaignsDirectory + '/' + campaign;
                 var fullPathToExperience = pathToCampaign + '/' + experience + '/';
                 if(teaser.campaignPath == pathToCampaign){
                     if(teaser.path.startsWith(fullPathToExperience) || teaser.thumbnail.startsWith(fullPathToExperience)){
                         return true;
                     }
                 }
                 return false;
             }
             
             for (i = 0; i < allTeasers.length; i++) {
                 if (isForcedTeaser(allTeasers[i], campaignName, experienceName)) {
                     var forcedTeaser = allTeasers[i];
                     forcedTeaser.name = "default";
                     forcedTeaser.segments = undefined;
                     delete forcedTeaser.segments;
                     allTeasers = [forcedTeaser]; 
                 }
             }
         }
	 
             CQ_Analytics.Engine.loadTeaser({ targetID: "_content_www_en_us_home_jcr_content_main-par_columncontainer_5696", teasers: allTeasers, strategy: "", trackingURL: null});
	 });
    </script>

                 var pathToCampaign = campaignsDirectory + '/' + campaign;

             function isForcedTeaser(teaser, campaign, experience){

                 var pathToCampaign = campaignsDirectory + '/' + campaign;
                 var fullPathToExperience = pathToCampaign + '/' + experience + '/';

         if (campaignName && experienceName){
             function isForcedTeaser(teaser, campaign, experience){
                 var campaignsDirectory = '/content/campaigns';
                 var pathToCampaign = campaignsDirectory + '/' + campaign;
                 var fullPathToExperience = pathToCampaign + '/' + experience + '/';
                 if(teaser.campaignPath == pathToCampaign){
                     if(teaser.path.startsWith(fullPathToExperience) || teaser.thumbnail.startsWith(fullPathToExperience)){
                         return true;
                     }
                 }
                 return false;
             }
             
             for (i = 0; i < allTeasers.length; i++) {
                 if (isForcedTeaser(allTeasers[i], campaignName, experienceName)) {
                     var forcedTeaser = allTeasers[i];
                     forcedTeaser.name = "default";
                     forcedTeaser.segments = undefined;
                     delete forcedTeaser.segments;
                     allTeasers = [forcedTeaser]; 
                 }
             }
